<section id="content" class="full-width">
					<div id="post-4899" class="post-4899 page type-page status-publish hentry">
			<span class="entry-title rich-snippet-hidden">RStudio Release Notes</span><span class="vcard rich-snippet-hidden"><span class="fn"><a href="https://www.rstudio.com/rviews/author/billrstudio-com/" title="Posts by bill@rstudio.com" rel="author">bill@rstudio.com</a></span></span><span class="updated rich-snippet-hidden">2018-10-29T17:45:33-04:00</span>						<div class="post-content">
				<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling"  style='background-color: rgba(255,255,255,0);background-position: center center;background-repeat: no-repeat;padding-top:0px;padding-right:30px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:30px;'><div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row "><div  class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion_builder_column_1_1 fusion-builder-column-1 fusion-one-full fusion-column-first fusion-column-last 1_1"  style='margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;'>
					<div class="fusion-column-wrapper" style="background-position:left top;background-repeat:no-repeat;-webkit-background-size:cover;-moz-background-size:cover;-o-background-size:cover;background-size:cover;"   data-bg-url="">
						<div class="fusion-text"><h2>RStudio v1.1.463 &#8211;Â October 29th, 2018</h2>
<p>This is a maintenance release of RStudio which contains fixes for the following issues:</p>
<ul>
<li>Fix sign-out issue when &#8220;stay signed in&#8221; is checked in RStudio Server (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1538">#1538</a>)</li>
<li>Fix hang when submitting empty passwords and password encryption is turned off (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1545">#1545</a>)</li>
<li>Fix dark theme partial application in data viewer when upgrading from 1.0 (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1573">#1573</a>)</li>
<li>Fix overlap between Refresh icon and plot title text (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1585">#1585</a>)</li>
<li>Fix slow File Open dialog on RStudio Desktop for Linux (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1587">#1587</a>)</li>
<li>Fix slow open of new files on Windows when using network drives (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1592">#1592</a>)</li>
<li>Fix build pane freeze when Rcpp::compileAttributes results in parse errors (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1601">#1601</a>)</li>
<li>Fix issue when migrating from RStudio 1.0 which could result in empty R files (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1623">#1623</a>)</li>
<li>Fix incorrect output type when compiling R script to non-HTML report (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1631">#1631</a>)</li>
<li>Improve spacing in account when username and servername are short (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1637">#1637</a>)</li>
<li>Fix incorrect background highlighting after reindent (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1643">#1643</a>)</li>
<li>Fix autocompletion of Rcpp C++ objects (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1654">#1654</a>)</li>
<li>Better &#8220;hand&#8221; cursor position on RStudio Desktop for Linux (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1659">#1659</a>)</li>
<li>Fix segfault that can occur when a notebook contains a Rcpp chunk with compilation failures (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1668">#1668</a>)</li>
<li>Fix problems with Git for Windows installations into sub-directories of home directory (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1679">#1679</a>)</li>
<li>Fix crashes when restarting R session while using a network drive (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1690">#1690</a>)</li>
<li>Don&#8217;t suspend R sessions with active external pointer objects (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1696">#1696</a>)</li>
<li>Allow new &#8220;Copy To&#8221; command in Files Pane to overwite its target (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1722">#1722</a>)</li>
<li>Respect &#8220;Load All&#8221; command shortcut when the Terminal is open (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1723">#1723</a>)</li>
<li>Detect full-screen mode correctly in Terminal pane (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1725">#1725</a>)</li>
<li>Support Pandoc 2 in RSTUDIO_PANDOC (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1756">#1756</a>)</li>
<li>Allow installation of package dependencies from repos not named CRAN (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1762">#1762</a>)</li>
<li>Fix password entry in Subversion and other shell dialogs (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1810">#1810</a>)</li>
<li>Ensure R Markdown files are saved before publish (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1821">#1821</a>)</li>
<li>Reconnect terminal when disconnected via proxy timeout (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/1844">#1844</a>)</li>
<li>Closing Shiny apps no longer can crash RStudio Server (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2061">#2061</a>)</li>
<li>Avoid hang when .git folder own Windows is not hidden (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2141">#2141</a>)</li>
<li>Setting non-default Knit Directory no longer breaks R Markdown websites (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2158">#2158</a>)</li>
<li>Fix scrolling through database objects if there are more than 25 (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2211">#2211</a>)</li>
<li>Pressing F1 on help autocompletions no longer raises an error (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2261">#2261</a>)</li>
<li>RTools 3.5 compatibility (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2636">#2636</a>)</li>
<li>R Notebook compatibility with R 3.5 (<a href="https://www.github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2748">#2748</a>)
<li>Fix issues with RStudio bundled with Anaconda in Windows 10 build 1803+ (<a href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2802">#2802</a>)</li>
<li>Fix disconnects with latest version of Shiny, RStudio Server, and Firefox (<a href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/2940">#2940</a>)</li>
<li>Fix paged table output R Notebooks with R 3.5.1 (<a href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/3163">#3163</a>)</li>
<li>Fix republishing content from directories with very short names (<a href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/3168">#3168</a>)</li>
<li>Fix locale issues on MacOS Mojave (<a href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/issues/3587">#3587</a>)</li>
<li>Server Pro: Update embedded nginx to 1.14.0</li>
<li>Server Pro: Can now log in to load-balanced servers when password contains a space (Pro #338)</li>
<li>Server Pro: Fix error when loading session on previously crashed server (Pro #619)</li>
</ul>
<h2>Previous Release Notes</h2>
</div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle"><a data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-4899-1" data-target="#a6bf2bbe16d71cc83" href="#a6bf2bbe16d71cc83"><div class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper"><i class="fa-fusion-box"></i></div><div class="fusion-toggle-heading">RStudio v1.1 - October 9, 2017</div></a></h4></div><div id="a6bf2bbe16d71cc83" class="panel-collapse collapse "><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<div id="highlights" class="section level3">
<div id="highlights" class="section level3">
<h3>Connections</h3>
<ul>
<li>New Connections tab for working with a wide variety of data sources</li>
<li>Connections to data sources are saved and can be easily reconnected and reused</li>
<li>Objects inside data sources can be browsed and contents viewed inside RStudio</li>
<li>Works with ODBC data sources and Spark, and can integrate with other R packages</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-terminal" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#terminal" aria-hidden="true"></a>Terminal</h3>
<ul>
<li>New Terminal tab for fluid shell interaction within the IDE</li>
<li>Support for xterm emulation including color output and full-screen console apps</li>
<li>Support for multiple terminals, each with persistent scrollback buffer</li>
<li>Web links in terminal can be clicked and opened in default browser (new tab for server)</li>
<li>Windows terminal supports multiple terminal shell types
<ul>
<li>Git Bash, if installed</li>
<li>Command Prompt (cmd.exe), 32-bit and 64-bit depending on OS support</li>
<li>PowerShell, 32-bit and 64-bit depending on OS support</li>
<li>Bash on Windows Subsystem for Linux, if installed on 64-bit Windows 10</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Default Windows terminal shell type set in new Global Options/Terminal preferences pane</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-object-explorer" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#object-explorer" aria-hidden="true"></a>Object Explorer</h3>
<ul>
<li>New view for the exploration of hierarchical / deeply-nested R objects</li>
<li>Can recursively inspect R lists, environments, functions, S4 objects</li>
<li>Integration with the xml2 package for exploration of XML documents</li>
<li>Generate R code that can be used to access a particular item within object</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-themes" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#themes" aria-hidden="true"></a>Themes</h3>
<ul>
<li>New flat, modern UI theme</li>
<li>New dark theme option</li>
<li>Retina-quality icons throughout</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-data-import" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#data-import" aria-hidden="true"></a>Data Import</h3>
<ul>
<li>Add support for all file encodings supported by R</li>
<li>Restore text import dialog from previous releases (uses only base R functions)</li>
<li>Code generator in import dialog now creates a relative path to data file</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-r-markdown" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#r-markdown" aria-hidden="true"></a>R Markdown</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added option to specify the working directory when executing R Markdown chunks</li>
<li>Added option to set preview mode (in viewer, window, etc.) in YAML header</li>
<li>Added option to skip knitting before publishing in YAML header</li>
<li>Multiline strings in YAML header are now properly highlighted</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-r-notebooks" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#r-notebooks" aria-hidden="true"></a>R Notebooks</h3>
<ul>
<li>Python chunks now respect virtualenv if present</li>
<li>&#8216;Rename in Scope&#8217; now works within R chunks</li>
<li>Global chunk options (e.g. &#8216;echo&#8217;) now properly respected in Notebook mode</li>
<li>Fixed an issue where non-R chunk output could become duplicated</li>
<li>Added option to set notebook mode in the document&#8217;s YAML header</li>
<li>Allow setting default chunk connection option to raw connection object</li>
<li>Added an &#8216;Use paged tables&#8217; checkbox under chunk options popup</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-git-integration" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#git-integration" aria-hidden="true"></a>Git Integration</h3>
<ul>
<li>Add support for creating new Git branches and setting upstream remotes</li>
<li>Git branch list is now searchable</li>
<li>RStudio warns when attempting to commit large files (&gt;10 MB)</li>
<li>Implemented &#8216;ignore whitespace&#8217; option for Git Diff view</li>
<li>Wait for index.lock file to clear before performing git operations (with recovery)</li>
<li>Improve handling of paths containing special characters</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-miscellaneous" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#miscellaneous" aria-hidden="true"></a>Miscellaneous</h3>
<ul>
<li>ANSI escape code support in console for colored output</li>
<li>Add support for custom, user-providedÂ <a href="https://rstudio.github.io/rstudio-extensions/rstudio_project_templates.html">project templates</a></li>
<li>Add support for middle-click pasting using X11 global selection (Linux Desktop only)</li>
<li>Document cursor position is now saved and restored between RStudio sessions</li>
<li>Addins are now fully searchable in dropdown toolbar menu</li>
<li>Add support for changing editor tabs with the mouse wheel</li>
<li>Snippets can now be inserted in the R console</li>
<li>Add option to knit in current working directory or project directory</li>
<li>Cmd/Ctrl+Enter in Help pane now sends selected example code to console</li>
<li>View(vignette(&#8230;)) now opens editor with vignette source</li>
<li>Ctrl+P/Ctrl+N to visit previous/next console history line (like readline)</li>
<li>Ctrl+R to search console history incrementally (like readline)</li>
<li>New &#8220;Copy To&#8221; command in Files pane to copy and rename in one step</li>
<li>Added UI for loading &#8216;.rds&#8217; files when clicked in Files pane</li>
<li>F2 in source editor opens data frame under cursor in a new tab</li>
<li>Highlight markdown inside ROxygen comments</li>
<li>Minor fixes to C++ syntax highlighting</li>
<li>Added syntax highlighting for TOML files</li>
<li>Provide autocompletion support for R6 &#8216;new()&#8217; methods</li>
<li>Improve performance of autocompletion for installed packages</li>
<li>Add option to run multiple consecutive lines of R with Ctrl+Enter</li>
<li>Add commands to run a line, statement, or consecutive lines</li>
<li>Add Clear Console button to top of Console pane</li>
<li>Add option to wrap around when navigating to previous or next editor tab</li>
<li>Allow opening directories as projects (Server and macOS only)</li>
<li>Vim: UseÂ <code>]f</code>Â andÂ <code>[f</code>Â to open adjacent files on the file system</li>
<li>Show disambiguation in overflow list when two editor tabs have the same filename</li>
<li>Respect control characters in error output; makes e.g. curl output correct</li>
<li>Add new cheat sheet links to Help: Data Import, Interfacing Spark</li>
<li>macOS: Always show project label on dock tiles</li>
<li>Remove 100 column limit in data viewer</li>
<li>Make columns in data viewer resizable</li>
<li>Add option to kill child processes when session exits</li>
<li>Upgrade toÂ <a href="http://pandoc.org/">pandoc</a>Â 1.19.2.1</li>
<li>Remove Packrat package sync notifications; replace with Check Library Status command</li>
<li>Add support for ligature coding fonts in RStudio Desktop for Windows and Linux</li>
<li>Added page viewer (accessible via getOption(&#8220;page_viewer&#8221;)) for viewing web content in an external window.</li>
<li>Add editor theme Dracula (thanks toÂ <a href="https://github.com/inventionate">Fabian Mundt</a>)</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add option to disable file uploads</li>
<li>Server Pro: Upgrade to TurboActivate 4.0; improves licensing</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add support for floating (lease-based) licenses</li>
<li>Server Pro: Show the size of suspended sessions</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add user-defined session labels</li>
<li>Server Pro: Upgrade to nginx 1.12.0</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add support for NFSv4 Access Control Lists in Project Sharing</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add support for user-initiated session quit and force-terminate</li>
<li>Server Pro: Add support for admin-supplied notifications in R sessions</li>
<li>Server Pro: New session-timeout-kill-hours option to expire and cleanly remove old R sessions</li>
</ul>
<h3><a id="user-content-bug-fixes" class="anchor" href="https://github.com/rstudio/rstudio/blob/v1.1/NEWS.md#bug-fixes" aria-hidden="true"></a>Bug Fixes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Fixed an issue where dragging tabs out multiple times could revert contents to older version</li>
<li>macOS: fixed &#8216;crash on wake&#8217; issue with late-2016 Macbooks</li>
<li>Fixed mangling of YAML header string values containing backticks</li>

<li>Git/SVN menu on global toolbar with commands for active file and project</li>
<li>Added history, zoom, and export for static HTML widgets in Viewer pane</li>
<li>View/Blame on GitHub commands for GitHub projects (file or selection driven)</li>
<li>Display current Git branch in main window title</li>
<li>Added stringsAsFactors and string.na options to Import Dataset</li>
<li>Restore previously entered input to console after executing commands</li>
<li>Increase limit on active plots from 30 to 100</li>
<li>Added documentation on which version rstudio package functions were introduced</li>
<li>Updated GWT library to version 2.6.0</li>
<li>Updated pdf.js for improved performance and fidelity of PDF preview</li>
<li>R 3.2: Use new API for accessing tools::httpdPort</li>
<li>R 3.2: Support for Rtools 3.2</li>
</ul>
<h3><strong>Bug Fixes</strong></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Package Development</strong></h3>
<p>This release includes a variety of tools to support R package development, including:</p>
<ul>
<li>A new Build tab with various package development commands and a view of build output and errors</li>
<li>Build and Reload command that rebuilds the package and reloads it in a fresh R session</li>
<li>Incremental reload is very fast and preserves the state of the previous R session, providing quick turnarounds and much more interactive workflow for package development</li>
<li>Additional commands for checking packages and building source and binary packages</li>
<li>Ability to create a new package based on existing R source files</li>
</ul>
<p>There are also a number of features aimed at making it easier to write R documentation:</p>
<ul>
<li>Preview and optional automatic preview on save for Rd files</li>
<li>Spell-checking for Rd files</li>
<li>Syntax highlighting, code-completion, and re-flowing forÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://roxygen.org/">Roxygen</a>Â comments</li>
<li>Ability to automatically invoke Roxygen prior to package builds</li>
</ul>
<p>There is also integration with theÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="https://github.com/hadley/devtools">devtools</a>Â package, including:</p>
<ul>
<li>Load All command and keyboard shortcut (Ctrl+Shift+L) that callsÂ <code style="color: #dd1144;">devtools::load_all</code></li>
<li>All package installations respect the development library established byÂ <code style="color: #dd1144;">devtools::dev_mode</code></li>
<li>Automatic restoration ofÂ <code style="color: #dd1144;">devtools::dev_mode</code>Â when reloading and restarting R sessions</li>
</ul>
<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Rcpp</strong></h3>
<p>This release includes many new features to support seamless R and C++ integration usingÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://dirk.eddelbuettel.com/code/rcpp.html">Rcpp</a>, including:</p>
<ul>
<li>Syntax highlighting for C/C++</li>
<li>Quick navigation to gcc errors and warnings</li>
<li>Support forÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://dirk.eddelbuettel.com/code/rcpp/Rcpp-attributes.pdf">Rcpp Attributes</a>:
<ul>
<li>Command w/ keyboard shortcut forÂ <code style="color: #dd1144;">Rcpp::sourceCpp</code></li>
<li>Editor support for embedded R code chunks in C++ source files</li>
<li>Automatic calls toÂ <code style="color: #dd1144;">Rcpp::compileAttributes</code>Â for package builds</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>New project option to create &#8220;Package w/Rcpp&#8221;</li>
<li>Automatic unloading of Windows dynamic libraries before package builds</li>
<li>Editor support for Rcpp code chunks in R Markdown</li>
</ul>
<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Source Editor</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>Find and Replace improvements:
<ul>
<li>Incremental search</li>
<li>Find/Replace in selection</li>
<li>Backwards find</li>
<li>Options for whole word and wrap</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Automatic indentation improvements:
<ul>
<li>Full support for auto-indent in Sweave/knitr code chunks</li>
<li>More intelligent handling of closing braces</li>
<li>Recognize operators (e.g. &#8216;+&#8217; for ggplot) as expression continuations</li>
<li>Option to control whether function arguments are vertically aligned</li>
<li>Option to disable auto-indent after pasting code into editor</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vim_(text_editor)">Vim</a>Â editing mode</li>
<li><a style="color: #0088cc;" href="https://github.com/chriskempson/tomorrow-theme#readme">Tomorrow</a>Â suite of editor themes</li>
<li>Surround selected text with quote/brace/paren/etc. on key input</li>
<li>Jump to matching brace/param (Ctrl+P)</li>
<li>New options: show whitespace, show indent guides, non-blinking cursor</li>
<li>Advance to next line after executing a selection from the editor</li>
<li>Significantly improved file-type detection (automatically open all files detected as text)</li>
</ul>
<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Console</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>More intelligent history navigation with up/down arrow keys</li>
<li>Confirm if attempting to quit while R console is busy</li>
<li>Improved auto-scroll behavior in the console</li>
<li>Option to focus console after executing code from editor</li>
<li>Send interrupt for ESC key even if server doesn&#8217;t appear to be busy</li>
<li>Display error output in distinct color for TextMate theme (and some others)</li>
</ul>
<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Plots</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>Plot zoom window improvements:
<ul>

<li>Remembers and restores it&#8217;s size (within each session)</li>
</ul>
</li>

<li>Always use native R png device with cairo bitmapType on Linux</li>
<li>Default plot export dialogs to current size of plots pane</li>
<li>Option to use cairo_pdf for PDF plot export on platforms where it is available</li>
<li>Set useDingbats = FALSE for PDF plot export (for compatibility with broader set of PDF viewers)</li>
<li>Compatibility with R Graphics Engine version 10 (R-devel)</li>
</ul>
<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Packages</strong></h3>
<ul>

<li>Warn and offer optional restart when updating packages that are currently loaded</li>
<li>Display package version and tooltip indicating which library they are installed in</li>

<li>Install rstudio and manipulate packages in default user library (R 3.0)</li>

<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Workspace</strong></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight: bold;"><strong>Sweave/knitr</strong></h3>

<li>browseURL can now open HTML documents now prefaced by the file:// protocol</li>
<li>browseURL in desktop mode no longer performs additional URL encoding</li>
<li>Ensure that PDF preview works even when concordance isn&#8217;t available</li>
<li>Display search results when looking up help term with more than one matching symbol</li>
<li>PDF links now open correctly from the Help pane</li>
<li>Always use bundled gnu grep on windows (rather than other versions of grep that might be in the path)</li>
<li>Eliminate upstart and AppArmor mis-detection on Debian testing</li>
<li>Prevent freeze when loading large line-wrapped source files on Chrome for Linux</li>

<li>Correct display of manipulate panel when Plots pane is on the left</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle"><a data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-4899-1" data-target="#72030a2ddc4af525c" href="#72030a2ddc4af525c"><div class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper"><i class="fa-fusion-box"></i></div><div class="fusion-toggle-heading">RStudio v0.93 â April 11th, 2011</div></a></h4></div><div id="72030a2ddc4af525c" class="panel-collapse collapse "><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<h2>New Features</h2>
<h3>Source editor enhancements</h3>
<p>We&#8217;ve added some new features &amp; options to the source editor. We&#8217;ve also received lots of feedback on more advanced capabilities users want in the editor and we will definitely address this in upcoming releases. New stuff in the editor includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Highlight all instances of selected text</li>
<li>Insert spaces for tabs (soft-tabs)</li>
<li>Customizable print margin line</li>
<li>Selected line highlight</li>
<li>Toggle line numbers on/off</li>
<li>Optional soft-wrapping for R source files</li>
</ul>
<p>The docs onÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/using/customizing#editing">source code editing options</a>Â include more details.</p>
<h3>Customizable layout and appearance</h3>
<p>One of the most frequently requested features we&#8217;ve have is the ability to put the Console and Source views side-by-side. This configuration (and others) are now possible. New appearance and layout options include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Customize locations of panes and tabs</li>
<li>Change default font size for code views</li>
<li>Select from various editor themes including TextMate, Eclipse, and others.</li>
</ul>
<p>For more details see the docs onÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/using/customizing#appearance">appearance and layout options</a>.</p>
<h3>Interactive plotting (manipulate)</h3>
<p>This release includes a package called manipulate that can be use to create interactive plots within RStudio. Manipulate is very flexible and includes the following capabilities:</p>
<ul>
<li>Generate plots with inputs bound to custom controls (rather than being hard-coded to a single value)</li>
<li>Variety of control types including slider, picker, and checkbox.</li>
<li>Controls appear next to the plot and can be easily shown and hidden</li>
</ul>
<p>More details as well as screenshots with examples can be found in theÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/advanced/manipulate">manipulate documentation</a>.</p>
<h3>Works with R installed from source</h3>
<p>The first beta of RStudio was compatible with the binary version of R distributed from CRAN. The current release works with any version of R, including:</p>
<ul>
<li>R built and installed from source using make install</li>
<li>MacPorts or Homebrew versions of R on MacOS X</li>
</ul>
<p>The docs onÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/advanced/versions_of_r">using different versions of R</a>Â describe how RStudio determines which R to run against on each platform.</p>
<h3>Character encoding</h3>
<p>In this release we&#8217;ve significantly improved handling of non-ASCII characters, this includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Unicode characters can be used for input and output in the console.</li>
<li>The source editor supports Unicode characters and can open/save files using any character encoding.</li>
<li>A product-wide default encoding can be set, and can be overridden on a per-document basis.</li>
</ul>
<p>See theÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/advanced/encoding">character encoding</a>Â documentation for more details.</p>
<h3>Improved management of working directories</h3>
<p>We&#8217;ve added a number of new features to make it easier to switch between working contexts located in different directories. These include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Option to specify a default initial working directory</li>
<li>Tools &#8211; Change Working Dir menu command to change both the working directory and Files pane.</li>
<li>Optional file associations for .RData and .R that initialize RStudio within the opened file&#8217;s directory</li>
<li>Windows: Startup in working directory specified for shortcuts</li>
<li>Mac: Startup in folder dragged and dropped on RStudio Dock icon</li>
<li>Linux: Startup in terminal working directory when run from the command line</li>
</ul>
<p>The docs onÂ <a style="color: #0088cc;" href="http://www.rstudio.com/ide/docs/using/workspaces">working directories and workspaces</a>Â go into more depth on these features.</p>
<h2>Other Enhancements</h2>
<h3>Console</h3>
<ul>
<li>Recognize \r character in console so that txtProgressBar works as expected</li>
<li>Lift restrictions on size of console input which can be sent to R (was 4K total, is now 4K per line)</li>
<li>Jump to next non-blank line in source after executing via Ctrl-Enter</li>
</ul>
<h3>Source Editing</h3>
<ul>
<li>Improved size and legibility of default fonts on Windows &amp; Linux</li>
<li>New keyboard shortcuts:
<ul>
<li>Alt- for inserting assignment (&#8220;&lt;-&#8220;) operator.</li>
<li>Ctrl+Shift+Home/End for select to start/end</li>
<li>Ctrl+Shift+P for Compile PDF</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Add &#8220;return&#8221; to list of symbols syntax highlighted as a keyword</li>
</ul>
<h3>Compatibility</h3>
<ul>
<li>Compatible with R 2.11.1 on Mac (previously required R 2.12)</li>
<li>Added CFBundleSignature to Mac version</li>
<li>Correctly initialize memory.limit to available physical memory on 64-bit Windows</li>
<li>Ensure that R uses Internet2 on Windows for interoperability with proxy servers.</li>
<li>Compatibility with changes to the R 2.13 internal web server (pass headers to custom handlers).</li>
<li>Allow RStudio desktop to run under root account</li>
<li>Improved support for openSUSE (still requires install from source):
<ul>
<li>Added install-dependencies-zypper script</li>
<li>Added init.d script for daemon management</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3>Packaging and Installation</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added RStudio.version function to show current version of RStudio</li>
<li>Changed name of RStudio binary from rdesktop to rstudio (avoid conflict with existing rdesktop binary)</li>
<li>Added /usr/bin/rstudio soft-link</li>
<li>Change DEB and RPM dependency on base R package to &#8220;recommends&#8221; rather than &#8220;depends&#8221;</li>
<li>Made it more straightforward to install from source:
<ul>
<li>Eliminated git pull requirement (can now build directly from tarball)</li>
<li>Optionally use system package manager installed versions of Qt4 &amp; Boost</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3>Miscellaneous</h3>
<ul>
<li>Added Tools menu with Interrupt R, Change Working Dir, and Options commands.</li>
<li>Add support for loading .rda files into Workspace.</li>
<li>Improved file icons including new custom icons for Rnw and Rd files.</li>
<li>Respect both R_USER and HOME environment variables for determining location of R home directory</li>
<li>Render plot changes on calls to Sys.sleep (enables animated plots)</li>
<li>Workaround Ubuntu TeX ~ substitution bug by using pdflatex rather than texi2dvi</li>
</ul>
<h2>Bug Fixes</h2>
<h3>Console</h3>
<ul>
<li>Workspace restored message prints at startup even if no workspace was restored</li>
<li>Numeric keypad Enter and navigation keys not correctly interpreted by console</li>
<li>Esc key not always correctly interpreted when attempting to exit from incomplete command.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Source Editing</h3>
<ul>
<li>Source pane can become fully selected and impossible to unselect.</li>
<li>Control-Enter to execute sometimes results in selection not updating properly</li>
<li>Jump to Word (Ctrl+Right) doesn&#8217;t navigate past &#8216;[&#8216; character.</li>
<li>Ctrl+Backspace doesn&#8217;t delete previous word on Windows</li>
<li>Characters illegible when Lucida Grande is installed on Mac systems</li>
<li>Active tab in source mode sometimes hidden or partially obscured</li>
<li>Control+S repeats last Undo/Redo on Firefox 3.6</li>
<li>Print from source view not working in Firefox 4</li>
<li>Eliminate key binding conflicts for international keyboard layouts</li>
<li>Incorrect shortcut key displayed in tooltip for Run from source commands</li>
<li>Variables with dots (&#8220;.&#8221;) in their names not highlighting on double-click.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Plotting</h3>
<ul>
<li>Graphics device not reselected after closing other device (e.g. pdf or png device)</li>
<li>X11 device and rgl package not working properly on on Mac.</li>
<li>Save as PNG command not working on Linux</li>
<li>Re-entrant plot rendering routine causes crash for plots which take a long time to be rendered.</li>
<li>plotmath expressions not rendered correctly</li>
<li>Plot history can grow arbitrarily large and cause disk/memory problems.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Compatibility</h3>
<ul>
<li>rJava package not working on Linux due to incomplete LD_LIBRARY_PATH</li>
<li>Not always correctly detecting whether TeX is installed</li>
<li>Dependency on psmisc package not specified for RStudio Server</li>
<li>Incorrect file association for download of RPM on Fedora</li>
</ul>
<h3>Miscellaneous</h3>
<ul>
<li>Failed to start when running behind some proxy server configurations.</li>
<li>Unable to initialize from .Rhistory file that is owned by root</li>
<li>Exit delay of 2-3 seconds in Mac version</li>
<li>Crash when custom gtk theme contains missing or invalid images for standard icons</li>
<li>Unresponsiveness when viewing extremely large data frames</li>
<li>Conflicting RStudio instances running in parallel if launched from different executable paths</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-clearfix"></div>

					</div>
				</div></div></div>
							</div>
												</div>
	</section>

			</main>  <!-- #main -->
